 ''patna ke puraane sachivalay main jahaan rajak baithte hai, vahaan se bamushkil saat kimi kii duuri par unka vidhansabha kshetra phulwari sharif he
 Here, like Fatehpur and Mahakar, anti-nitish sentiments are widespread among Mahadalits
 isi kshetra ke dhibra-shahpur ilaake ke dainik majuri karne vaale 45 varshiya lala maanjhi kehete hai, ''aap aise aadmi ke bare main kya kah sakate hai, jo aapke aage thali parosata he or jaise hi aap khaanaa shuru karte hai, vah thali khinch letaa he? nitish kumaar ne to yahi kiya he
 Nitish Kumar could not digest how a Mushar-rat eater and a pig-grader would become more popular than him
 ''maanjhi kabhi dhibra nahin aae hai, magar nitish vahaan pahunche hai
 On 15 August, he went to hoist the tricolor in the Dalit colony and gave a speech
 lekin dhibra ke mahadalit nivaasiyon ko yaad nahin aata ki nitish ne kabhi unki dasha sudhaarney ke liye kuch kiya ho
 In his mind, Nitish's image is of the leader who drove Manjhi out
 aise main phulwari sharif main jedy (you) ke liye kitni sambhaavna he or vah kitni surakshit he? phulwari sharif main rajak ke khasmkhas 57 varshiya ajay sinha kehete hai, ''mantri ji abhi bhi aasaani se jeet jaaenge

 main mahadalit voton ko lekar aashwast nahin hum
 "at the moment no one seems confident about these votes
 donon hi bade gathbandhanon kaa bhagya abhi adhar main hi lataka hua he

 lekin jeet or haar kii disha to isi se tay hogi
 Yoga guru Baba Ramdev was caught on camera on Thursday with BJP candidate Mahant Chandnath saying that do not talk about money when the mic is on
 mahant ne pehle ramdev se kaha tha ki alvar sansadeey kshetra main chunaav prachaar ke dauraan unhen dhan kii kami ho rahi he
 The conversation, which took place just before the press conference began on Thursday, was recorded on camera as his mic was on
 sammelan se kuch hi kshan pehle mahant ne ramdev se kaha ki unhen dhan laane main dikkat ho rahi he jisapar yoga guru ne unhen chetaya ki mike on hone par dhan kii baat naa karo

 ’ alvar se bijepi pratyaashee mahant ne ise bhampa or muskura die

 C
 mittal ne netaaon ke khilaaf praathmiki darj karne or mahant ko ayogy qaraar dene kii maang kii he
 The central government has sought a report from the UP government regarding the suspended IAS officer Durga Shakti Nagpal
 vahiin, sutron kaa kahana he ki rajya sarkaar ne nilamban waapas lene ke bajaay esadm ko chargeshit dene kaa man bana liya he or jawaab talab kiya jayega
 According to sources, if the government is not satisfied with the response to the charge sheet, then further action will be taken
 is maamle main kendriya mantri narayansami ne kaha he ki durga kaa paksh bhi sarkaar jaanegi
 Narayanasamy has said that if wrong action is taken on Durga then the Center will interfere
 upi sarkaar ne greater noida main tainaat iees durga shakti nagpal ko suspend kar diya
 The government cited the reason that Durga was negligent in demolishing the wall of a mosque, while opposition parties said that Durga was suspended under the pressure of the sand mafia as she was taking action against the sand mafia
 idhar, durga shakti ke nilamban par ab raajnneeti bhi tej ho gai he
 Mayawati attacked the Akhilesh government of UP and said that there is goonda and mafia rule in UP
 unhone kaha ki mining mafia kii pole kholane kii sajaa ek eemaandaar iees afasar durga shakti nagpal ko jhelni pad rahi he
 The comments congress or bijepi ne bhi durga ke nilamban ko galat bataate hue unhen phir se behaal karne kii maang kii he
 At the same time, Shivpal Yadav, senior minister of the UP government, says that Durga's suspension has nothing to do with the mining mafia
 unhone kaha ki yah kahana galat hoga ki unhen eemaandaaree kii sajaa mili he
 In this case, Union Minister Narayanasamy has said that the government will also go to Durga's side
 narayansami ne kaha he ki agar durga par galat karrwai hui he tab centre dakhal degaa
 UP government suspended IAS Durga Shakti Nagpal posted in Greater Noida
 sarkaar ne vajah bataai ki ek masjid kii diwaar giraane main durga ne laaparvaahee barti, jabaki vipakshi dalon kaa kahana he ki durga ko ret mafia ke dabaav main suspend kiya gaya kyonki vah ret mafia ke khilaaf karrwai kar rahi thim
 Here, politics has also intensified due to the suspension of Durga Shakti
 mayawati ne upi kii akhilesh sarkaar par hamalaa bolte hue kaha ki upi main gunda or mafia raaj he
 He said that an honest IAS officer Durga Shakti Nagpal is going to face the punishment of opening the pole of the mining mafia
 tippaniyan The Congress and BJP have also called for Durga's suspension to be reinstated, denying her suspension

 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh on Thursday called for more discipline in government spending and said that India's financial deficit is 'too high' and is hampering domestic and foreign investment
 28 oktober ko cabinet main pherbadal ke baad apane sarkari awaas par 77 sadasyeey mantriparishad ke saath apni pehali baithak main pradhanmantri ne vishwa kii taaja aarthik tasviir pesh kii, jo bhartiya arthvyavastha ko prabhavit kar rahi he
 He also shared some thoughts on the government's agenda
 manmohan singh ne kaha, "kathin vaishvik aarthik sthiti kaa asar ham par bhi ho rahaa he
 As a result, our growth rate has declined, exports have come down and the fiscal deficit is increasing
 " He said, "our main concern is about the fiscal deficit, which is very high and is hindering domestic and foreign investment
 ye mudde samoochee arthvyavastha or kai vibhaagon ke kaaryon ko prabhavit kar rahe hai, jinke pratinidhi yahaan maujuud hai
 " pradhanmantri kii is tippanee se do din purv kendriya vittamantri pi chidambaram ne vittiya ghaataa kam karne ke liye ek panchavarshiya yojana kii ghoshnaa kii thi
 He aimed to bring it down to three per cent by FY 2016-17, reducing the fiscal deficit to 5 per cent in 2011-12
 8 fisadi darj kiya gaya

 *** Exposure to air pollution even for a short time may increase the risk of miscarriage
 ek nae adhyayan main yah chintit karne vaali baat saamne ai he
 Air pollution is associated with all the bad effects on health, from asthma to premature delivery
 america ke uta vishvavidhyalay ke anusandhankartaaon ne paaya ki uta rajya kii sabase adhik aabaadi vaale kshetra main rahane vaali mahilaayein jab vaayu pradooshan kaa str badhane ke baad uske sampark main ain to unamem garbhpaat hone kaa khatra zyada (16 pratishat) bad gaya
 The study, conducted from 2007 to 2015, included 1300 women who went to the emergency department for medical help after an abortion (up to a 20-week pregnancy)
 anusandhankartaaon kii team ne hawa main teen saadhaaran pradooshak tatwon - atisookshm kanon (piem 2
 5), after increasing the amount of nitrogen oxide and ozone, the risk of miscarriage was tested over a period of three to seven days
 is team ne paaya ki nitrogen oxide ke bade str ke sampark main aane vaali mahilaon ko garbhpaat hone kaa khatra 16 pratishat tak bad gaya
 The study is published in the journal Fertility and Sterility
